< Text>
DO NOT ACCEPT ANYTHING MORE THAN AN OIL CHANGE. See attached photos for proof.

Just laying out facts, and debating if I can take legal action:

My car has been 100% perfect up until I visited this location. Never had any problems beyond having to occasionally blow air into my tires.

1. Just moved to Oakland and looked for the nearest Jiffylube for an oil change
2. Jiffylube staff offered to clean my battery. Given it's covid, I figured they could use the extra cash so for the first time, I said okay.
3. They completely removed my battery and went to town spraying whatever fluids they have into my engine bay. Is Jiffylube supposed to completely remove the battery? I thought they were going to only wipe the discharge.
4. 2hours later they are finally done, but I am having trouble starting my car. The dashboard looks like a Christmas tree with all of the warnings lit up
5. They tell me to go to Pepboys down the street because their obd2 reader is not working and return tomorrow to speak to Jiffylube's manager, Mohamed
6. Pepboys mentioned that it is likely something wrong with the battery and that it may need to be replaced
7. I returned the next day to speak with Mohamed, who took a look and tried to avoid any blame. Leaving me to go figure it out on my own. This interaction added no value to me and was a waste of my time.
8. I go back to Pepboys. They tell me I need a new battery, and that I have the following obd2 codes: po560 & p0606
9. p0606 has to do with the Power Train Control Module and costs an additional $500-$1500 (based on google) to have replaced.

Overall, for a simple oil change, this specific location has cost me $500 so far with up to an additional $1500 to replace the PCM. As well as 5hours driving around and waiting for repairs.

My car is not the same. If you think I can take action - I could use some guidance. Otherwise, I might just make this a major learning lesson never to go to Jiffylube again.

Already spoke with Philip Arnold and that didn't prove to go anywhere. So I am cutting my losses and was referred to a trusted local auto mechanic to handle all of my car needs moving forward. cheaper too.

I will let you, the reviewer, figure out the quality of service here.<//Text>

The food here is pretty good and consistent in how it is made or at least tastes. Which I personally like because you know it's gonna always taste the same. <rating>2</rating><Time>1481498048449<//Time><Review>This is less a review of L&L than a review of this individual L&L. Ever since I was first taken to an L&L on O'ahu I've been a big fan, and now frequent one that is close to my home. This particular L&L doesn't hold a candle to the rest. Yes they have mostly the same menu, though some items have been covered over with white cardboard, nothing I ordered was of the same quality. The bbq chicken was fatty and some bites tasted fainty like balogna, the rice was mushy, and even the macaroni salad tasted off. I dont know if wasn't fresh or they failed to follow the recipe.  I also ordered steam vegetable which was mostly cabbage. I considered ordering katsu but when i saw there katsu sauce it was more red than brown and to me that said way to much ketchup. I probably should have realized it wasnt as good as the whole time i was there only myself and the two staff were present. If you are in the mood for hawaiian bbq this place is edible, maybe even ok to those who dont know any better, but if you do maybe keep driving.< /Review><Name>Mathew Mitchell</Name></record>

<Rate>3< /Rate>< review>
I'm giving a 3 for overall experience (food and service). I purchased the 12 piece family meal and the 5 piece shrimp meal. I will breakdown each item as follows:

Chicken - Seasoned well. Taste was good.
Shrimp - Seasoned well. Taste was good.
Parmesan Lime Corn - Overall taste was just okay.
Macaroni and Cheese - Not Impressed.
Honey Biscuits - Good.

For the amount of time I spent waiting awkwardly for my meal (there isnt anywhere to sit)  to be completed I expected my food to be hot. It was lukewarm at best. The setup is basically a liquor/convenience store with a 711 type food set up. There is not a dedicated Krispy Krunch worker. So be prepared to wait as the cashier handles the liquor/convenience store customers in between taking your order. Oh and they also sell ice cream but it didn't look appealing since the majority looked like it was melted.

My recommendation would be to call before going in. I may order chicken and biscuits from them again but I'm cool on the sides.</review>

<Review>No compassion. No understanding. Sad example for human kindness and interaction. This business has no empathy for you or your pet. Their staff is more concerned with their own schedules than for the safety and comfort of your pet.

Backstory:

I was in LA picking up a puppy from LAX. The process took much longer than expected and we did not get the dog until later. The poor puppy had been delayed so long she had soiled her crate and herself. We cleaned her up as best we could and drove to the Pet Wash. We arrived 30 mins before they closed, but 30 mins after their imposed "no self bath" rule.

Given the circumstances and the fact that we had a 6 hour drive home, we begged and pleaded with the staff of the Pet Wash (there were about 5 people just standing about) to allow us to wash off this poor puppy. We offered to clean up the tub and area and even to pay 4x the cost of the bath. We offered to validate our story with airbill receipts so they knew we weren't BS'ing them.

The staff refused and turned us away.

We were forced to buy gallons of water from the 711 and try to wash her as best we could in the parking lot.

Never have I experienced such callous disregard from a business that caters to animals.

Had this been you, would you have helped an animal in need? I know I  would have.

I don't live in the area, so I don't have to threaten to take my business elsewhere. I hope someone who reads this will do that for me. People who are more concerned about some dumb rule rather than helping a suffering animal do not deserve your patronage.

THIS BUSINESS DOES NOT CARE. TAKE YOUR MONEY ELSEWHERE.< /Review></record>

We had our wedding at Legacy Ballroom almost a month ago, and it was ABSOLUTELY WONDERFUL! The venue is beautiful, and their food is AMAZING! Special thanks to the chef!

When planning the wedding, we did not have a coordinator, so we had to find all vendors and organize and coordinate everything on our own. Everyone told us that we won‚Äôt be able to plan a wedding and have a successful stress-free day without a coordinator. But we are stubborn and determined, so we went on to do everything on our own (and we succeeded).

The event manager (Yervand) was extremely helpful and supportive throughout the whole process. He was responsive by phone and email, and was always happy to answer numerous questions and give advice. What stood out to us at this venue, compared to many others that we have toured (it was probably at least 6 more), was their levels of professionalism and care. On the day of the wedding, all our vendors and staff at Legacy really went above and beyond their duties and coordinated amongst each other, and we had zero problems (even without a coordinator)! It was a fantastic day!

< text>
Looking for a wedding venue was overwhelming. There are so many options and not enough information readily available online to narrow the choice. When I submitted an inquiry online to Legacy Ballroom, I got an email with Yervand's name and phone number. He was immediately available for a phone call, and not only answered many of my questions about having a wedding reception at Legacy Ballroom, but also helped me brainstorm through some of the other options I had come across so far. He was honest, professional, and gave me great advice.

Soon after, we visited the venue for the first time while searching for the right one. It is beautiful - even when it wasn't fully decorated for any upcoming event! The base decor is elegant, the LED screens throughout the venue are so impressive and can bring any ambiance you envision to life. After seeing the venue and meeting Yervand in person, Legacy instantly moved to the top of our list.

While planning for our own wedding, we also had the opportunity to be a guest at a wedding at Legacy earlier in the year, and got to experience the venue from a guest's point of view. The food from Anoush catering is delicious, the banquet hall looked even more beautiful with the lighting and florals, and the service was professional all night.

Throughout the year, Yervand checked in with us multiple times and we met with him every so often to go over questions, requests, and discuss how to make our November wedding unique to our vision and needs. Yervand is always professional, fun to work with, and ensured that we were getting the optimal services within our budget. What can be a stressful experience, went smoothly from start to finish with the help of a great team at LA Banquets!</text>

<Date>1549234370867< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating><review>One of the most daunting tasks any newly engaged couple can take on is to plan their wedding. There are thousands of details to consider and a thousand more you didn't even know existed. Fortunately, Nara and I gave ourselves 2 years to plan our wedding and almost two months into our engagement, we had already booked Legacy Ballroom for our reception. It was a no-brainer: the venue was newly remodeled, they had a state-of-the-art lighting/visual system, we already knew just how sophisticated and delicious Anoush Catering at Legacy Ballroom was, and the staff was incredibly professional with everything from setting up appointments, drawing up an itemized contract, all while exercising a completely transparent business model that kept us in the loop for every single dollar we were spending. Our event manager Yervand was a natural: he knew exactly how to actualize our dream wedding, made the perfect recommendations for us, and made sure that everything we signed up for was in our best interest and not for the business. Even when we were looking for outside vendors for things like a party bus, a travel agency for our honeymoon, and breakfast burritos, Yervand had a recommendation for it all (and we ended up booking through all of his recommendations--also that brisket breakfast burrito from Coffee Commissary is fire). I'm happy to say we've found ourselves a lifelong friend with Yervand, not just a professional relationship.

To all of the brides and grooms who are searching around for a venue, here are our takeaways:

- We were at capacity but at no time did it feel cramped.
- Yes, there's a lot of food brought out, but it's all delicious and it ensures that every palate is pleased.
- When in doubt, don't be afraid to defer to your event manager. I promise, they're on your side.
- Get the short rib. Shh. This is non-negotiable.
- Don't worry about ANYTHING on your big day, all details have already been outlined at Legacy and everything will be done exactly the way you want it.
- Get the short rib.
- Did I mention how perfect everything was? I mean, seriously.
- Do yourselves a favor and get the bridal suite to just hang out in, relax, eat, and drink before your grand entrance. They even have a monitor in there so you can keep an eye on how full the venue is getting!

Only a week has passed since our wedding, but we can't stop talking about it. Thank you to the entire staff at Legacy Ballroom, special shout outs to Yervand and Arthur, you guys are truly incredible people.

<Rate>1</Rate>< text>
DON'T FALL FOR THEIR BAIT-AND-SWITCH ADVERTISING!!!
I made an appointment with Stanton Optical because they were advertising a great deal: an eye exam and 2 pairs of glasses, all for $78. What they don't tell you until you're in there is that the special price only applies to the "value" glasses. The "value" glasses are a very small selection, and all super-ugly frames. If you want to actually look decent, you'll have to pay full price. I was unpleasantly surprised to learn this, but the "full price" listed on a lot of the frames was about $50, an amount I can handle, so I went ahead and chose a couple pairs. My unpleasant surprise continued when I found out at the VERY END of my visit there, that the prices listed on the frames is ONLY for the frames, and they charge an additional $200 to install the lenses!!
I ended up paying over $300 altogether (even with their BOGO). I went ahead and paid it against my better judgment, because by that point I had been in there for HOURS and needed to get home and relieve my babysitter. I regretted my decision, and contacted Stanton Optical the next day to arrange to return the glasses for a refund, and to get a copy of my prescription so I could purchase glasses elsewhere. I called 3 or 4 separate times that day, and nobody was willing to help me. I was either left on hold for a half hour, or told to call back later.
I'm extremely unhappy with Stanton Optical's failure to disclose their pricing in an upfront and honest fashion, and downright disgusted with their failure to provide any customer service over the phone the following day. There are tons of optometrists out there, do yourself a favor and pick a better one.<//text>
